    SUPPORTING EXHIBITS
      (M-1, 0-1, RF-1, P-1, R-1, & C-1)
          Office of Budget   -   2025
The estimated cost of this report for the
Department of the Navy (DON) is $8,307.

The estimated total cost for supporting the DON
budget justification material is approximately
$3,070,790 during the 2024 fiscal year. This
includes $199,436 in supplies and $2,871,355 in
labor.
